***sijpelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sijpelen.html>sijpelen</a> (44661)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A frequentative with <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-elen</i> of early modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">sijpen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to drip</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sīpen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sīpaną</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">seep</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*seib</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*sib-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pour out, drip, trickle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sēbum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">suet, tallow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">εἴβω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">eíbō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to drop, drip</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sijpelen.html>sijpelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to trickle, seep</li></ol>

***sikkel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sikkel.html>sikkel</a> (44660)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sikle</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sichel</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">secula</i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sīcīlis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sickle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, through a Western <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sikilō</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Sichel</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sikkel.html>sikkel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sikkel.html>sikkels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sikkel.html>sikkeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>sickle</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sind.html>sind</a> (88188)</h1><br></body> 
***sinds.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sinds.html>sinds</a> (478)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:sint.html>sint</a></i>, with a <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a> <i>-s</i>. The form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a nasal variant of Germanic <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sīþiz</i>, also found in Old High German <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href = vnd.unilang:sint.html>sint</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to some, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:sint.html>sint</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> instead shortened from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sīdent</i>, which itself <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> related with Old English <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">siþþan</i> and Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">síðan</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup> This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, however, improbable because <i><a href = vnd.unilang:sint.html>sint</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> already found in the oldest <a href = vnd.unilang:stages.html>stages</a> of both Dutch and German. Modern Dutch <i><a href = vnd.unilang:sinds.html>sinds</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> therefore, in all likelihood, just an indirect cognate of the similar sounding English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">since</i>. The onset <i>s-</i> (instead of expected <i>z-</i>) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> due to a prepositioned <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, thus <i>*<a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> zinds</i> → <i>*tzinds</i> → <i><a href = vnd.unilang:sinds.html>sinds</a></i>. Immediately cognate with Luxembourgish <i class="Latn mention" lang="lb">zanter</i>. Also cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">seit</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">since</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sinds.html>sinds</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>since
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sedert.html>sedert</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<ul><li><a href = vnd.unilang:sedert.html>sedert</a></li></ul>

</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:vanaf.html>vanaf</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sinds.html>sinds</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vorige.html>vorige</a> week <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rome.html>Rome</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vertrok.html>vertrok</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gezien.html>gezien</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***singing.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:singing.html>singing</a> (63012)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">syngyng</i>; equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sing</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/singing" class="extiw" title="w:singing"><a href = vnd.unilang:singing.html>singing</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/singing" class="extiw" title="w:singing">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:singing.html>singing</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">singings</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The act of using the voice to produce musical <a href = vnd.unilang:sounds.html>sounds</a>; vocalizing.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Disclosing information, or giving evidence about another.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A gathering for the purpose of <a href = vnd.unilang:singing.html>singing</a> shape note <a href = vnd.unilang:songs.html>songs</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:singing.html>singing</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:singing.html>singing</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:singing.html>singing</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Smooth and flowing.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of a kettle etc.</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Producing a whistling sound due to the escape of steam.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:singing.html>singing</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sing</i></span></span></li></ol>
</body>

</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sinterklaasavond.html>sinterklaasavond</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sinterklaasavond.html>sinterklaasavonden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sinterklaasavond.html>sinterklaasavondje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>The evening with presents, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> on the day of Sinterklaas, 6 December (in Belgium) or the day before (in the Netherlands).</li></ol>

***sire.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sire.html>sire</a> (3282)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:sire.html>sire</a></i>, the nominative singular of <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">seignor</i>; from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">senior</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">senex</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">senior</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:seigneur.html>seigneur</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">seignior</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>sir</a></i><span class="serial-comma">,</span><span class="serial-and"> and</span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:monsieur.html>monsieur</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sire.html>sire</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">sires</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A lord, master, or other person in authority, most commonly used vocatively: formerly in speaking to <a href = vnd.unilang:elders.html>elders</a> and superiors, <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> only when addressing a sovereign.</li>
<li>A male animal; a stud, especially a horse or dog, that <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> fathered another.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A father; the head of a family; the husband.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1591–1592</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_VI,_Part_3" class="extiw" title="w:Henry VI, Part 3">The Third Part of <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> the Sixt,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="with the Death of the Duke of Yorke">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. William Shakespeares Comedies, <a href = vnd.unilang:histories.html>Histories</a>, amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a>: Published <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to the True Originall <a href = vnd.unilang:copies.html>Copies</a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London |  Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act III, scene ii]:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">And raise his issue, like a loving <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sire.html>sire</a></b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A creator; a maker; an author; an originator.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Shelley and provide title, author's full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd>[He] <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sire.html>sire</a></b> of an immortal strain.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sire.html>sire</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">sires</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">siring</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">sired</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of a male</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to procreate; to father, beget, impregnate.
<ul><li><b>1994</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nelson_Mandela" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Nelson Mandela">Nelson Mandela</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Long_Walk_to_Freedom" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Long Walk to Freedom">Long Walk to Freedom</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:abacus.html>Abacus</a> 2010, p. 6:
<dl><dd>In these travels, my father <b>sired</b> thirteen children in all, four boys and nine <a href = vnd.unilang:girls.html>girls</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:sire.html>sire</a></b> 
</p>
<ol><li>aanspreektitel <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koning.html>koning</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:keizer.html>keizer</a></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sirena</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">serene</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">sereine</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sirēna</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">Sīrēn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Σειρήν</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Seirḗn</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sirene.html>sirene</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sirenen.html>sirenen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sirenes.html>sirenes</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sirene.html>sirenetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A siren, a dangerous nymph of Greek mythology, luring passers-by using an irresistible song</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A seductive but dangerous female</li>
<li>(<i>plural <a href = vnd.unilang:sirenes.html>sirenes</a></i>) A siren, a noisy warning device</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:siroop.html>siroop</a> (20465)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:siroop.html>siroop</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">sirop</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">siruppus</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">syrupus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">شَرَاب</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šarāb</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a>, beverage, wine, coffee, syrup</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">شَرِبَ</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šariba</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sorbet.html>sorbet</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sherbet</i>.
Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">sirop</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">siroppo</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">jarabe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">jarope</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Portuguese_language" class="extiw" title="w:Portuguese language">Portuguese</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pt">xarope</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sissy.html>sissy</a> (23333)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sis.html>sis</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-y</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sissy.html>sissy</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">sissies</b>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An effeminate boy or <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>.</li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">BDSM</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A male crossdresser who adopts feminine behaviours.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote?)</span>, Paul Zante, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:sissy.html>Sissy</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dreams.html>Dreams</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:motel.html>Motel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sissy.html>Sissy</a></i> (page 4)

Yes, I <a href = vnd.unilang:knew.html>knew</a> it would from watching <a href = vnd.unilang:videos.html>videos</a> of <b>sissies</b> being spanked by their dominant mistresses.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Sister.
<ul><li><b>2008</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:rita.html>Rita</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>T</a>. Kohn, ‎William Lynwood Montell, <i>Always a People: Oral <a href = vnd.unilang:histories.html>Histories</a> of Contemporary Woodland Indians</i>

He wouldn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> leave; he stayed, too. He kissed her, <a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a> her hand, <a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a> her he would miss her.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

Compare piss; wee-wee.
</p>

***sixties.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sixties.html>sixties</a> (41557)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sixties.html>sixties</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">plural of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sixty</i></span></span></li></ol>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sixties.html>sixties</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative letter-case form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sixties.html>Sixties</a></i></span></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">The decade of the 1860s, 1960s, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>The decade of one's life from age 60 through age 69.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">temperature<span class="ib-comma">,</span> rates<span class="ib-comma">,</span> plural only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The range between 60 and 69.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Highs in the mid <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sixties.html>sixties</a></b>.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">1960s</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">'60s</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">60s</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sixties.html>sixties</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>From or evoking the 61st through 70th years of a century (chiefly the 1960s).
<dl><dd><i>She coughed as she exhaled. <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sixties.html>Sixties</a></b> weed <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> nowhere near this strong.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1993</b>,  Arthur Marwick,  “Six <a href = vnd.unilang:novels.html>Novels</a> of the <a href = vnd.unilang:sixties.html>Sixties</a> — Three French, Three Italian”, in  <cite>Journal of Contemporary History</cite>, volume 28, number 4, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Digital_object_identifier" class="extiw" title="w:Digital object identifier">DOI</a>:<span class="neverexpand"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://doi.org/10.1177%2F002200949302800401">10.1177/002200949302800401</a></span></small>, page 588:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Historians do not rely on single <a href = vnd.unilang:bits.html>bits</a> of evidence, but are always seeking corroboration, qualification, correction. These <a href = vnd.unilang:novels.html>novels</a>, set in context, are in themselves interesting fragments of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sixties.html>sixties</a></b> culture.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<ul><li>This spelling and pronunciation <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> mostly used by Jews and others who are familiar with the Hebrew term. Non-Jews more commonly use <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sabbat.html>sabbat</a></i>.</li></ul>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">schachern</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to haggle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">סחרן</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sakhern</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to trade</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sjacheren.html>sjacheren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to sell a pup, to swindle with substandard wares, to scam.
<ul><li><b>2012</b>, Arthur <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Amerongen, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:mambo.html>Mambo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jambo.html>Jambo</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:krankzinnige.html>krankzinnige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:liefde.html>liefde</a> in Zuid-Amerika</i>, Nijgh amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>Van</a> Ditmar.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:centrum.html>centrum</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Paraguay <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:overstroomd.html>overstroomd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <i>indígenas</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:allemaal.html>allemaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dezelfde.html>dezelfde</a> meuk <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sjacheren.html>sjacheren</a></b>.
<dl><dd>The city centre of Paraguay <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> swamped by <i>indígenas</i> who all <b>try to sell a pup</b> with the same <a href = vnd.unilang:shit.html>shit</a>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>to wrangle
<ul><li><b>2015</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:elle.html>Elle</a> Eggels, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:achtste.html>achtste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zuster.html>zuster</a></i>, The House of Books.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leerde.html>leerde</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:sjacheren.html>sjacheren</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:prijs.html>prijs</a>.
<dl><dd>I learnt how to <b>wrangle</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> prices.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sjamaan.html>sjamaan</a> (23016)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">шама́н</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šamán</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Evenki_language" class="extiw" title="w:Evenki language">Evenki</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="evn">шама̄н</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="evn-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">şamān</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First mentioned in 1714:
</p>
<ul><li><b>1714</b>, Cornelis <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bruin.html>Bruin</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:reizen.html>Reizen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> Moskovie, <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> Persie <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> Indie</i>, publ. by Wetstein, Oosterwyk amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Gaete, page 11.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>Onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hen.html>hen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> iemant, dienze den naem <a href = vnd.unilang:geven.html>geven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <i><b>Sjaman</b></i> of <i>Koedieſnick</i>, houdende <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hunnen.html>hunnen</a> Prieſter, of <a href = vnd.unilang:liever.html>liever</a> Toveraer, <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> geloovende <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> hy <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alle.html>alle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geluk.html>geluk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ongeluk.html>ongeluk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorzeggen.html>voorzeggen</a>:</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Among them <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> someone, whom they give the name of <i><b>Shaman</b></i> or <i>Kudisnick</i>, holding him for their priest, or rather sorcerer, and believing that he can predict all fortune and misfortune to them:</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sjees.html>sjees</a> (99837)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:chaise.html>chaise</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sjees.html>sjees</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sjezen.html>sjezen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sjees.html>sjeesje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:chaise.html>chaise</a></span>; a high, open (sometimes convertible), two-wheeled carriage.</li></ol>
